id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_body" class="ajax__tab_body ajax__scroll_vert"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="visibility: visible;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures_ProductFeatureDesc">Expanse M4 Carbine 5.56mm NATO/.223 Remington 16.1 Inch Barrel Matte Black Finish A2 Front Sight Adjustable Stock 30 Round Mag<p></p> <p>Chambered in 5.56x45 NATO with a 16.1 inch barrel with 1:7 inch right hand rifling. Adjustable stock. Thirty round aluminum magazine. Flat top receiver ready to add your own accessories. A2 front sight.</p> <p>The Expanse M4 puts a Colt quality AR-15 within easy reach of the modern sportsman looking to enhance his or her collection, or the first-time buyer looking for a starting point on which to build their dream modern sporting rifle. Either way, the Expanse M4 in 5.56 x 45 NATO (.223 Rem.) is a great way to add another Colt to the stable.</p> <p><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/colt/colt-098289026019-1.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="198"><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/colt/colt-098289026019-4.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="360"><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/colt/colt-098289026019-3.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="360"><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/colt/colt-098289026019-2.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="228"><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/colt/colt-098289026019-5.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="312"></p></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications_ProductsSpecifications"><ul> <li>Name : Expanse M4 5.56mm 16 30+1</li> <li>Desc : </li> <li>Model : Expanse M4</li> <li>Model # : CE1000</li> <li>Manufacturer : Colt</li> <li>Caliber : 223 Rem | 5.56 NATO</li> <li>Type : Rifle</li> <li>Action : Semi-Auto</li> <li>Barrel : 16.1"</li> <li>Capacity : 30+1</li> <li>Finish : Matte</li> <li>Length : 32"-35.5"</li> <li>Receiver : Matte Black</li> <li>Magazine : 1 / 30 rd.</li> <li>Weight : 6.44 lbs.</li> </ul></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Reviews"> <div id="Review"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_UpdatePnlProductReviewDetails"> <div class="Sorting"> <span class="TitleStyle"> Reviewed by <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_CustomersCnt">2</span> customer </span>&nbsp; <span> <select name="ctl00$ctl00$MainContent$uxProduct$uxProductTabs$ProductTabs$pnlCustomerReviews$uxProductReviews$RateList" onchange="javascript:setTimeout('__doPostBack(\'ctl00$ctl00$MainContent$uxProduct$uxProductTabs$ProductTabs$pnlCustomerReviews$uxProductReviews$RateList\',\'\')', 0)" id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_RateList" class="SortByDropdown"> <option selected="selected" value="desc">Newest First</option> <option value="asc">Oldest First</option> <option value="5">Highest Rating First</option> <option value="1">Lowest Rating First</option> </select> </span> </div> <div> <table id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_ReviewList" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;"> <tbody><tr> <td class="ReviewItem"> <div class="ItemStyle"> <div class="Title"> <span class="Subject"> The perfect gun</span>, June 23, 2016</div> <div class="Content"> <div class="StarRating"> <img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"></div> <div class="Row"> Gets the job done! Handles very well in both palms. The perfect gun for a novice shooter. Very accurate and fun! No kickback. Great range gun!</div> <div class="Row"> By <span class="Text"> Frank</span> from <span class="Text"> Dearborn MI</span></div> </div> </div> </td> </tr><tr> <td class="ReviewItem"> <div class="ItemStyle"> <div class="Title"> <span class="Subject"> Gotta give the Colt Expanse a thumbs up!</span>, April 08, 2016</div> <div class="Content"> <div class="StarRating"> <img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"></div> <div class="Row"> Anybody remembering the low cost Colt 6900 two years ago, don't think the Expanse is the same thing. Instead it's basically the highly regarded Colt 6920 minus a chrome linied barrel. And the ejection port cover, the forward assist and H buffer (which can be added for about $50). The lower receiver is the same as the 6920 except for a lightened match trigger and the lighter buffer. Most of the difference is the upper - the non-chrome lined barrel and missing dust cover and forward assist. There also may be less testing of the bolt but it still is a good unit. Otherwise, the goodness of the Colt 6920 is there, the civilian version of the military M4 but a few hundred bucks cheaper. Definitely check out the Expanse, read the reviews and go handle one. It offers a lot for the money, a better package than the similarly priced S&amp;W M&amp;P-15 Sport and Ruger AR-556. And the best thing - it isn't marked Expanse, it's rollmarked M4 Carbine, Cal. 5.56mm. You could drop a BCM upper on the lower and go off to war while the Expanse upper perks along on a PSA lower defending the home front. Or keep it complete, it's a great AR for the price.</div> <div class="Row"> By <span class="Text"> Quentin</span> from <span class="Text"> Boise</span></div> </div> </div> </td> </tr> </tbody></table> </div> <div class="Paging"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_topNavigation"> <a id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_TopPrevLink" disabled="disabled"> Previous</a> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_lblPagingInfo"> | PAGE1 of 1 | </span> <a id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_TopNextLink" disabled="disabled">Next </a> </div> </div> <div class="Spacer"> &nbsp;</div> <div> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_lblErrorMsg"></span></div> <div class="Spacer"> &nbsp;</div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> <!-- Right Content --> <div class="RightContent" itemprop="offers" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Offer"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_UpdPnlOrderingOptions"> <div class="OrderingOptions"> <div id="Attributes"> </div> <div id="Add-Ons" align="right"> </div> <!--Information : If you change Add-Ons <div> tag ID [EX:<div ID ="Add-Ons">] , then you need to update that name in this javascript [File:"thumbnailviewer.js"] on line no :43 and 111.
